                    function SpaceNameFth(lcStName) {

                        var spaceWrd = parseInt(lcStName.indexOf(" "));
                        var lcStNameWrd = lcStName;

                        if (/\s/.test(lcStName)) {

                            var wrd1 = String(lcStNameWrd).substring(0, spaceWrd);
                            var wrd2 = String(lcStNameWrd).substring((spaceWrd + 1), String(lcStNameWrd).length);
                            var cadena = wrd1 + "<br />" + wrd2;

                        } else {

                            var cadena = lcStNameWrd;

                        }

                        return cadena;

                    }

			function cierra() {
				$("#chained").css("z-index", "1");

				for(i=0;i<21;i++)
				{
					$("#ops"+ i).css("display", "none");
				}

				$("#m1_op").css("display", "none");
				$("#s1_op").css("display", "none");
			}
	
        
        var altura = 369;
			
			function acomoda(cual) {

				var cuenta_altura = 0;
				var primero = 0;
				var cuenta_columnas = 1;

				if ($('#fops'+cual).html() == "") {

					var contefinal = "";

					contefinal += "<div style='float:left;width:250px'>";

					$('#ops' + cual + ' .col').each(function (i) {

						cuenta_altura += $(this).outerHeight();

						if (cuenta_altura > altura) {
							cuenta_columnas++;
							contefinal += "</div>";
							cuenta_altura = 0;
						}

						if (cuenta_altura == 0) {
							contefinal += "<div style='float:left;width:250px'>";
							cuenta_altura = 0;
						}

						contefinal += $(this).html();

						$(this).html('');

					});

					$('#ops' + cual).width((250 * cuenta_columnas)); //+150
					//$('#ops' + cual).height((cuenta_altura+70)); //
					
					$('#fops'+cual).html(contefinal);
				}

			}

    $("#srchProd").keyup(function(e){
            
			if(e.keyCode == 40){keydown(e.keyCode); return false;}
			
			var txt = $("#srchProd").val();

			 if (e.keyCode == 13) {    
			 
				if ($("#srchProd").val() != '') {
					//DCS 28Ene2014        
					window.location.href = 'http://buscador.sanborns.com.mx/search?client=Sanborns&output=xml_no_dtd&proxystylesheet=Sanborns&sort=date:D:L:d1&oe=UTF-8&ie=UTF-8&ud=1&exclude_apps=1&site=Sanborns&ulang=es&access=p&entqr=3&entqrm=0&filter=0&getfields=*&q=' + document.getElementById("srchProd").value;
					return false;
				}
			 
			 
			 }else{
			 
				 try{
                
                $.ajax({
                type: "GET",
                url: "../_layouts/wpSanborns/GSARequest.aspx",
				data: "term=" + txt,
                success: function (response) {
                   var succOk =  (JSON.parse(response)).results;
                    var i=1;
                    $("#ulSugg").html('');
                    document.getElementById("divSugg").style.visibility = "visible";
                    if( succOk.length > 0){
					    $("#ulSugg").append("<li id='liSugg' class='liSuggCss' ><a>Sugerencias</a></li>");
					    for (var l in succOk) {
						    $("#ulSugg").append("<li id='liSugg' class='liSuggCss' tabindex='"+ i +"'><a href=\"http://buscador.sanborns.com.mx/search?client=Sanborns&output=xml_no_dtd&proxystylesheet=Sanborns&sort=date:D:L:d1&oe=UTF-8&ie=UTF-8&ud=1&exclude_apps=1&site=Sanborns&ulang=es&access=p&entqr=3&entqrm=0&filter=0&getfields=*&q=" + succOk[l].name + "\">"+ succOk[l].name +"</a></li>");
					        i++;
                        }
					    $("#ulSugg").append("<li id='liSugg' class='liSuggCss' ><a onclick=\"CerrarSugg()\"><img id='imgClsSgs' src='/images/error.png' /></a></li>");

				    }else{
					    CerrarSugg();
				    }
		
                },
                complete: function (response) {
                //var compOk = response;
                },
                error: function (a, b, c) {
                //var resNO = response;
                }
            });    

            }catch(e){alert("Error: " + e)}
			 
			 
		 }

	});

    function CerrarSugg(){
        $("#ulSugg").html('');
        document.getElementById("divSugg").style.visibility = "hidden";
	}

	function keydown(e){  

		var $listItems = $("#ulSugg li");

		var key = e,
			$selected = $listItems.filter('.selected'),
			$current;

		if ( key != 40 && key != 38 ) return;

		$listItems.removeClass('selected');

		if ( key == 40 ) // Down key
		{
			if ( ! $selected.length || $selected.is(':last-child') ) {
				$current = $listItems.eq(1);
			}
			else {
				$current = $selected.next();
			}
		}
		else if ( key == 38 ) // Up key
		{
			if ( ! $selected.length || $selected.is(':first-child') ) {
				$current = $listItems.last();
			}
			else {
				$current = $selected.prev();
			}
		}

		$current.addClass('selected');
		 
		$("#srchProd").val($current[0].innerText);
		return false;
	}
